about_this_resource_text: "<p>Prof. Sontag discusses causal inference, examples of\
  \ causal questions, and how these guide treatment decisions. He explains the Rubin-Neyman\
  \ causal model as a potential outcome framework.</p>\r\n<p>Speaker: David Sontag</p>\r\
  \n            <p><a href=\"./resolveuid/ebe128ab8488bae8e6a7e6cab50a9033\">Lecture\
  \ 14: Causal Inference, Part 1 slides (PDF - 2.2MB)</a></p>\r\n"

  <span m="452690">practice,</span> <span m="453230">for</span> <span m="453350">example,</span>
  <span m="453770">to</span> <span m="454010">recognize</span> <span m="454670">that</span>
  <span m="454790">there</span> <span m="454970">is</span> <span m="455090">heterogeneity</span>
  <span m="455780">in</span> <span m="455870">treatment</span> <span m="456160">response,</span>
  <span m="457670">then</span> <span m="457820">we</span> <span m="457910">have</span>
  <span m="458060">to</span> <span m="458150">somehow</span> <span m="458870">change</span>
  <span m="459440">the</span> <span m="460520">question</span> <span m="461030">that</span>
  <span m="461180">we're</span> <span m="461300">asking.</span> <span m="464090">I'll</span>
  <span m="464150">give</span> <span m="464270">you</span> <span m="464360">one</span>
  <span m="464600">last</span> <span m="464900">example,</span> <span m="465930">which</span>
  <span m="466070">is</span> <span m="467210">perhaps</span> <span m="467540">a</span>
  <span m="467600">more</span> <span m="467720">traditional</span> <span m="468200">question</span>
  <span m="468680">of,</span> <span m="469220">does</span> <span m="469490">X</span>
  <span m="469730">cause</span> <span m="470060">y?</span> <span m="470600">For</span>

  <span m="660080">I</span> <span m="660230">thought</span> <span m="660870">causal</span>

  <span m="668720">to</span> <span m="669170">X2</span> <span m="670010">goes</span>

  <span m="673280">X4?</span> <span m="674490">Or</span> <span m="674960">I'll</span>
  <span m="675080">say,</span> <span m="675260">this</span> <span m="675410">is</span>
  <span m="675560">X1,</span> <span m="676250">that's</span> <span m="676550">X2,</span>

  <span m="679190">Or</span> <span m="679340">maybe</span> <span m="680330">the</span>

  <span m="685640">x4.</span> <span m="687970">And</span> <span m="688070">trying</span>
  <span m="688280">to</span> <span m="688370">distinguish</span> <span m="688880">between</span>
  <span m="689300">these</span> <span m="689450">different</span> <span m="689720">causal</span>
  <span m="690020">graphs</span> <span m="690440">from</span> <span m="690590">observational</span>
  <span m="691130">data</span> <span m="692710">is</span> <span m="692920">one</span>
  <span m="693220">type</span> <span m="693520">of</span> <span m="693610">question</span>

  <span m="694330">ask.</span> <span m="696840">And</span> <span m="696960">the</span>
  <span m="697050">one</span> <span m="697320">thing</span> <span m="697530">you</span>
  <span m="697680">learn</span> <span m="698220">in</span> <span m="698880">traditional</span>
  <span m="699660">machine</span> <span m="700020">learning</span> <span m="700230">treatments</span>
  <span m="700590">of</span> <span m="700680">this</span> <span m="700980">is</span>
  <span m="701190">that</span> <span m="701550">sometimes</span> <span m="702060">you</span>
  <span m="702150">can't</span> <span m="702330">distinguish</span> <span m="702840">between</span>
  <span m="703200">these</span> <span m="703350">causal</span> <span m="703650">graphs</span>
  <span m="704010">from</span> <span m="704160">the</span> <span m="704220">data</span>
  <span m="704400">you</span> <span m="704490">have.</span></p><p><span m="705210">For</span>
  <span m="705360">example,</span> <span m="705990">suppose</span> <span m="706350">you</span>
  <span m="706440">just</span> <span m="706620">had</span> <span m="706740">two</span>
  <span m="706980">random</span> <span m="707250">variables.</span> <span m="709050">Because</span>
  <span m="709770">any</span> <span m="710190">distribution</span> <span m="711090">could</span>
  <span m="711240">be</span> <span m="711300">represented</span> <span m="712410">by</span>
  <span m="713190">probability</span> <span m="714180">of</span> <span m="714630">X1</span>

  <span m="2706210">sensitivity</span> <span m="2706900">analysis.</span></p><p><span

  <span m="2708970">the</span> <span m="2709060">type</span> <span m="2709240">of</span>
  <span m="2709300">question</span> <span m="2709600">you</span> <span m="2709660">might</span>
  <span m="2709840">ask</span> <span m="2710200">is,</span> <span m="2710800">how</span>
  <span m="2711040">would</span> <span m="2711220">my</span> <span m="2711430">conclusions</span>
  <span m="2712120">have</span> <span m="2712300">changed</span> <span m="2712990">if</span>
  <span m="2713140">there</span> <span m="2713350">were</span> <span m="2713740">a</span>
  <span m="2713770">confounding</span> <span m="2714310">factor</span> <span m="2714890">which</span>
  <span m="2715060">was</span> <span m="2715270">blah</span> <span m="2715690">strong?</span>
  <span m="2717860">And</span> <span m="2718010">that's</span> <span m="2718190">something</span>
  <span m="2718400">that</span> <span m="2718520">one</span> <span m="2718700">could</span>
  <span m="2718820">try</span> <span m="2719060">to</span> <span m="2719630">answer</span>
  <span m="2719960">from</span> <span m="2720140">data,</span> <span m="2723210">but</span>
  <span m="2723650">it's</span> <span m="2723770">really</span> <span m="2724010">starting</span>
  <span m="2724340">to</span> <span m="2724400">get</span> <span m="2724490">beyond</span>
  <span m="2724730">the</span> <span m="2724820">scope</span> <span m="2725420">of</span>
  <span m="2725900">this</span> <span m="2726110">course.</span> <span m="2726510">So</span>
  <span m="2726620">I'll</span> <span m="2726740">give</span> <span m="2726890">you</span>
  <span m="2726950">some</span> <span m="2727070">readings</span> <span m="2727400">on</span>
  <span m="2727520">it,</span> <span m="2727580">but</span> <span m="2727750">I</span>

  <span m="2729350">lecture.</span> <span m="2732000">Now,</span> <span m="2732100">the</span>

  <span m="2737270">And</span> <span m="2737390">by</span> <span m="2737510">the way,</span>
  <span m="2737680">pay</span> <span m="2737860">close</span> <span m="2738070">attention</span>
  <span m="2738400">here</span> <span m="2738610">because</span> <span m="2741460">at</span>
  <span m="2741610">the</span> <span m="2741760">end</span> <span m="2742150">of</span>
  <span m="2742270">today's</span> <span m="2742660">lecture--</span> <span m="2743080">and</span>
  <span m="2743170">if</span> <span m="2743260">I</span> <span m="2743320">forget,</span>
  <span m="2743680">someone</span> <span m="2744010">must</span> <span m="2744220">remind</span>
  <span m="2744580">me--</span> <span m="2745030">I'm</span> <span m="2745180">going</span>
  <span m="2745390">to</span> <span m="2745540">ask</span> <span m="2746080">you</span>
  <span m="2746770">where</span> <span m="2747220">did</span> <span m="2747430">these</span>
  <span m="2747670">two</span> <span m="2747940">assumptions</span> <span m="2748510">come</span>
  <span m="2748780">up</span> <span m="2749650">in</span> <span m="2749950">the</span>
  <span m="2750040">proof</span> <span m="2750400">that</span> <span m="2750520">I'm</span>
  <span m="2750610">about</span> <span m="2750790">to</span> <span m="2750880">give</span>
  <span m="2751060">you.</span></p><p><span m="2753610">The</span> <span m="2753700">first</span>
  <span m="2753940">one</span> <span m="2754030">I'm</span> <span m="2754120">going</span>
  <span m="2754190">to</span> <span m="2754360">give</span> <span m="2754510">you</span>
  <span m="2754570">will be a</span> <span m="2754650">dead</span> <span m="2755100">giveaway.</span>
  <span m="2755370">So</span> <span m="2755470">I'm</span> <span m="2755530">going</span>
  <span m="2755650">to</span> <span m="2755710">answer</span> <span m="2756040">to</span>
  <span m="2756160">you</span> <span m="2756280">where</span> <span m="2756640">ignorability</span>
  <span m="2757060">comes</span> <span m="2757270">up,</span> <span m="2757840">but</span>
  <span m="2758140">it's</span> <span m="2758290">up</span> <span m="2758380">to</span>
  <span m="2758470">you</span> <span m="2758560">to</span> <span m="2758650">figure</span>
  <span m="2758860">out</span> <span m="2758980">where</span> <span m="2759140">does</span>
  <span m="2759270">common</span> <span m="2759510">support</span> <span m="2759880">show</span>
  <span m="2760060">up.</span> <span m="2761560">So</span> <span m="2761710">what</span>
  <span m="2761860">is</span> <span m="2761980">common</span> <span m="2762220">support?</span>
  <span m="2762670">Well,</span> <span m="2763350">what</span> <span m="2763500">common</span>
  <span m="2763780">support</span> <span m="2764260">says</span> <span m="2764890">is</span>
  <span m="2765130">that</span> <span m="2766960">there</span> <span m="2767140">always</span>
  <span m="2767560">must</span> <span m="2767800">be</span> <span m="2767950">some</span>
  <span m="2768280">stochasticity</span> <span m="2769450">in</span> <span m="2769570">the</span>
  <span m="2769630">treatment</span> <span m="2769960">decisions.</span> <span m="2771440">For</span>
  <span m="2771520">example,</span> <span m="2773450">if</span> <span m="2775080">in</span>
  <span m="2775230">your</span> <span m="2775350">data</span> <span m="2776440">patients</span>
  <span m="2776850">only</span> <span m="2777270">receive</span> <span m="2777630">treatment</span>
  <span m="2778080">A</span> <span m="2778770">and no</span> <span m="2779010">patient</span>
  <span m="2779400">receives</span> <span m="2779640">treatment</span> <span m="2780030">B,</span>
  <span m="2781780">then</span> <span m="2782290">you</span> <span m="2782410">would</span>
  <span m="2782500">never</span> <span m="2782740">be</span> <span m="2782830">able</span>
  <span m="2782950">to</span> <span m="2783040">figure</span> <span m="2783280">out</span>
  <span m="2783580">the</span> <span m="2783700">counterfactual,</span> <span m="2784420">what</span>
  <span m="2784570">would</span> <span m="2784690">have</span> <span m="2784780">happened</span>
  <span m="2785050">if</span> <span m="2785110">patients</span> <span m="2785380">receive</span>
  <span m="2785620">treatment</span> <span m="2785910">B.</span></p><p><span m="2789160">But</span>
  <span m="2789310">what</span> <span m="2789460">happens</span> <span m="2789730">if</span>
  <span m="2789820">it's</span> <span m="2789940">not</span> <span m="2790120">quite</span>
  <span m="2790360">that</span> <span m="2790510">universal</span> <span m="2791050">but</span>
  <span m="2791230">maybe</span> <span m="2791530">there</span> <span m="2791680">is</span>
  <span m="2791840">classes</span> <span m="2792430">of</span> <span m="2792490">people?</span>
  <span m="2794260">Some</span> <span m="2794530">individual</span> <span m="2794785">is</span>
  <span m="2795040">X,</span> <span m="2795370">let's</span> <span m="2795490">say,</span>
  <span m="2795640">people</span> <span m="2795910">with</span> <span m="2796030">blue</span>
  <span m="2796300">hair.</span> <span m="2797350">People</span> <span m="2797590">with</span>
  <span m="2797710">blue</span> <span m="2798040">hair</span> <span m="2799840">always</span>
  <span m="2800170">receive</span> <span m="2800440">treatment</span> <span m="2800770">zero</span>
  <span m="2802450">and</span> <span m="2802550">they</span> <span m="2802640">never</span>
  <span m="2802910">see</span> <span m="2803090">treatment</span> <span m="2803420">one.</span>
  <span m="2805200">Well,</span> <span m="2806460">for</span> <span m="2806670">those</span>
  <span m="2807000">people,</span> <span m="2807790">if</span> <span m="2808440">for</span>
  <span m="2808620">some</span> <span m="2808890">reason</span> <span m="2809340">something</span>
  <span m="2809760">about</span> <span m="2810000">them</span> <span m="2810270">having</span>
  <span m="2810570">blue</span> <span m="2810810">hair</span> <span m="2810990">was</span>
  <span m="2811200">also</span> <span m="2811710">going</span> <span m="2812040">to</span>
  <span m="2812190">affect</span> <span m="2812730">how</span> <span m="2812970">they</span>
  <span m="2813090">would</span> <span m="2813210">respond</span> <span m="2813600">to</span>
  <span m="2813660">the</span> <span m="2813750">treatment,</span> <span m="2814710">then</span>
  <span m="2814890">you</span> <span m="2815010">wouldn't</span> <span m="2815250">be</span>
  <span m="2815340">able</span> <span m="2815520">to</span> <span m="2815610">answer</span>
  <span m="2816060">anything</span> <span m="2816450">about</span> <span m="2816720">the</span>
  <span m="2816780">counterfactual</span> <span m="2817470">for</span> <span m="2817620">those</span>
  <span m="2817770">individuals.</span> <span m="2819660">This</span> <span m="2819960">goes</span>
  <span m="2820200">by</span> <span m="2820320">the</span> <span m="2820410">name</span>

  <span m="2821220">a</span> <span m="2821310">propensity</span> <span m="2821940">score.</span>
  <span m="2823560">It's</span> <span m="2824160">the</span> <span m="2824280">probability</span>
  <span m="2825090">of</span> <span m="2825300">receiving</span> <span m="2826050">some</span>
  <span m="2826320">treatment</span> <span m="2827310">for</span> <span m="2827580">each</span>
  <span m="2827760">individual.</span></p><p><span m="2829230">And</span> <span m="2829470">we're</span>
  <span m="2829680">going</span> <span m="2829920">to</span> <span m="2830040">assume</span>
  <span m="2831180">that</span> <span m="2831450">this</span> <span m="2831720">propensity</span>
  <span m="2832530">score</span> <span m="2833460">is</span> <span m="2833670">always</span>
  <span m="2834150">bounded</span> <span m="2834780">between</span> <span m="2835350">0</span>
  <span m="2835980">and</span> <span m="2836220">1.</span> <span m="2837150">So</span>
  <span m="2837570">it's</span> <span m="2837810">between</span> <span m="2838290">1</span>
  <span m="2838530">minus</span> <span m="2838770">epsilon</span> <span m="2839250">and</span>

  <span m="2840510">small</span> <span m="2840930">epsilon.</span> <span m="2843020">And</span>
  <span m="2843170">violations</span> <span m="2843890">of</span> <span m="2843950">that</span>
  <span m="2844100">assumption</span> <span m="2845330">are</span> <span m="2845450">going</span>
  <span m="2845840">to</span> <span m="2846020">completely</span> <span m="2846770">invalidate</span>
  <span m="2847370">all</span> <span m="2847490">conclusions</span> <span m="2848000">that</span>
  <span m="2848090">we</span> <span m="2848210">could</span> <span m="2848330">draw</span>
  <span m="2848510">from</span> <span m="2848690">the</span> <span m="2848780">data.</span>
  <span m="2850610">All</span> <span m="2850880">right.</span> <span m="2851520">Now,</span>
  <span m="2851760">in</span> <span m="2852120">actual</span> <span m="2852540">clinical</span>
  <span m="2852900">practice,</span> <span m="2854100">you</span> <span m="2854220">might</span>
  <span m="2854400">wonder,</span> <span m="2855190">can</span> <span m="2855330">this</span>

  <span m="2857340">there</span> <span m="2857490">are</span> <span m="2857730">clinical</span>
  <span m="2858150">guidelines.</span> <span m="2860880">Well,</span> <span m="2861380">a</span>

  <span m="2862280">where</span> <span m="2862460">you'll</span> <span m="2862640">see</span>

  <span m="2863270">follows.</span></p><p><span m="2863940">First,</span> <span m="2864320">often,</span>

  <span m="2871010">You</span> <span m="2871160">know</span> <span m="2871580">that</span>

  <span m="2880130">treatments.</span> <span m="2880490">And</span> <span m="2880580">right</span>

  <span m="2881720">really</span> <span m="2881990">know</span> <span m="2882170">which</span>
  <span m="2882410">one</span> <span m="2882590">to</span> <span m="2882680">try.</span>
  <span m="2883100">So</span> <span m="2883460">a</span> <span m="2883490">clinician</span>

  <span m="2885320">class.</span> <span m="2886340">And</span> <span m="2886490">if</span>
  <span m="2886580">that's</span> <span m="2886910">not</span> <span m="2887090">working,</span>
  <span m="2887390">you</span> <span m="2887480">try</span> <span m="2887690">a</span>

  <span m="2888670">so</span> <span m="2888800">on.</span> <span m="2889040">And</span>
  <span m="2889130">it's</span> <span m="2889220">a</span> <span m="2889280">bit</span>
  <span m="2889400">random</span> <span m="2889850">which</span> <span m="2890030">class</span>

  <span m="2893910">settings,</span> <span m="2894340">there</span> <span m="2894510">might</span>
  <span m="2894780">be</span> <span m="2894960">good</span> <span m="2895230">clinical</span>

  <span m="2906340">that</span> <span m="2906730">this</span> <span m="2907120">is</span>
  <span m="2907300">the</span> <span m="2907390">right</span> <span m="2907570">way</span>
  <span m="2907660">to</span> <span m="2907750">do</span> <span m="2907960">things,</span>
  <span m="2908350">and</span> <span m="2908860">clinicians</span> <span m="2909310">who

  <span m="2909910">east</span> <span m="2910180">coast</span> <span m="2910420">might</span>
  <span m="2910570">be</span> <span m="2910630">trained</span> <span m="2910930">that</span>
  <span m="2911170">this</span> <span m="2911500">is</span> <span m="2911620">the</span>
  <span m="2911710">right</span> <span m="2911860">way</span> <span m="2911950">to</span>
  <span m="2912070">do</span> <span m="2912250">things.</span> <span m="2913630">And</span>
  <span m="2913750">so</span> <span m="2915310">even</span> <span m="2915640">if</span>
  <span m="2915880">any</span> <span m="2916120">one</span> <span m="2916330">clinician's</span>

  <span m="2919360">way,</span> <span m="2920180">you'll</span> <span m="2920260">see</span>

  <span m="2923620">a</span> <span m="2923650">bit</span> <span m="2923800">subtle</span>
  <span m="2924130">how</span> <span m="2924250">to</span> <span m="2924340">use</span>
  <span m="2924700">that</span> <span m="2924940">in</span> <span m="2925030">your</span>
  <span m="2925150">analysis,</span> <span m="2925790">but</span> <span m="2925810">trust</span>
  <span m="2926050">me,</span> <span m="2926170">it</span> <span m="2926230">can</span>
  <span m="2926380">be</span> <span m="2926470">done.</span></p><p><span m="2929160">So</span>
  <span m="2929820">if</span> <span m="2929970">you</span> <span m="2930030">want</span>
  <span m="2930300">to</span> <span m="2930810">do</span> <span m="2931110">causal</span>
  <span m="2931440">inference</span> <span m="2931680">from</span> <span m="2931830">observational</span>
  <span m="2932340">data,</span> <span m="2933130">you're</span> <span m="2933180">going</span>
  <span m="2933290">to</span> <span m="2933360">have</span> <span m="2933600">to</span>

  <span m="3183430">could</span> <span m="3183570">we</span> <span m="3183670">possibly</span>
  <span m="3184030">compute</span> <span m="3184420">the</span> <span m="3184540">average</span>
  <span m="3184840">treatment</span> <span m="3185140">effect</span> <span m="3185560">from</span>
  <span m="3185800">data?</span> <span m="3187870">Remember,</span> <span m="3188310">average</span>
  <span m="3188450">treatment</span> <span m="3188760">effect,</span> <span m="3189430">mathematically,</span>
  <span m="3189960">is</span> <span m="3190050">the</span> <span m="3190110">expectation</span>
  <span m="3190740">between</span> <span m="3191340">potential</span> <span m="3191730">outcome</span>
  <span m="3192060">Y1</span> <span m="3192960">minus</span> <span m="3193320">Y0.</span></p><p><span
  m="3196860">The</span> <span m="3197100">key</span> <span m="3197520">tool</span>
  <span m="3197970">which</span> <span m="3198180">we'll</span> <span m="3198360">use</span>
  <span m="3198750">in</span> <span m="3198840">order</span> <span m="3198960">to</span>
  <span m="3199560">estimate</span> <span m="3199980">that</span> <span m="3200250">is</span>
  <span m="3200370">what's</span> <span m="3200550">known</span> <span m="3200730">as</span>
  <span m="3200850">the</span> <span m="3200970">adjustment</span> <span m="3201600">formula.</span>
  <span m="3202290">This</span> <span m="3202410">goes</span> <span m="3202590">by</span>
  <span m="3202920">many</span> <span m="3203130">names</span> <span m="3203400">in</span>
  <span m="3203460">the</span> <span m="3203550">statistics</span> <span m="3204000">community,</span>
  <span m="3204370">such</span> <span m="3204570">as the G-formula</span> <span m="3205230">as</span>
  <span m="3205320">well.</span> <span m="3206960">Here,</span> <span m="3207140">I'll</span>
  <span m="3207230">give</span> <span m="3207350">you</span> <span m="3207410">a</span>
  <span m="3207430">derivation</span> <span m="3207920">of</span> <span m="3208010">it.</span>
  <span m="3210460">We're</span> <span m="3210765">first</span> <span m="3211070">going</span>
  <span m="3211340">to</span> <span m="3211430">recognize</span> <span m="3212240">that</span>
  <span m="3213560">this</span> <span m="3213860">expectation</span> <span m="3214670">is</span>
  <span m="3214790">actually</span> <span m="3215060">two</span> <span m="3215570">expectations</span>
  <span m="3216230">in</span> <span m="3216320">one.</span> <span m="3216830">It's</span>
  <span m="3216980">the</span> <span m="3217040">expectation</span> <span m="3217850">over</span>
  <span m="3218120">individuals</span> <span m="3218840">X</span> <span m="3219770">and</span>
  <span m="3219890">it's</span> <span m="3219980">the</span> <span m="3220040">expectation</span>

  <span m="3222230">Y</span> <span m="3222650">given</span> <span m="3222950">X.</span>
  <span m="3223760">So I'm</span> <span m="3224000">first</span> <span m="3224270">just</span>

  <span m="3224900">it</span> <span m="3224990">out</span> <span m="3225200">in</span>

  <span m="4666580">here,</span> <span m="4667480">you</span> <span m="4667570">don't</span>
